<h4 id="flume+kafka+storm-flume" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-size:14px; line-height:1.42857; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<br>
</h4>
<h4 id="flume+kafka+storm-flume" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-size:14px; line-height:1.42857; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
flume</h4>
<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-原理" style="margin:10px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
原理</h5>
<div class="code panel pdl conf-macro output-block" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px">
<div class="codeContent panelContent pdl" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; line-height:20px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div id="highlighter_415389" class="syntaxhighlighter sh-confluence nogutter  java" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; width:1017px; position:relative; overflow:auto; font-size:1em">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1084px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; font-size:14px; min-height:inherit'>
<tbody style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">
<tr style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">
<td class="code" style='border:0px; background:0px center; overflow:visible; font-size:14px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 15px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1069px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; min-height:inherit'>
<div class="container" title="Hint: double-click to select code" style="margin:15px 0px 0px; padding:0px 0px 15px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:relative; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:pre-wrap">
<div class="line number1 index0 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Flume
 是一个可靠的，分布式的，用于采集，聚合，传输海量日志数据的系统。</code></div>
<div class="line number2 index1 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Flume
 的核心是把数据从数据源收集过来，再送到目的地。为了保证输送一定成功，在送到目的地之前，会先缓存数据，待数据真正到达目的地后，删除自己缓存的数据。</code></div>
<div class="line number3 index2 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>下面是一些概念.</code></div>
<div class="line number4 index3 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number5 index4 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Event</code></div>
<div class="line number6 index5 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>数据传输的基本单位.通常是一行记录.</code></div>
<div class="line number7 index6 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number8 index7 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Agent</code></div>
<div class="line number9 index8 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Flume的运行核心,有三个组件:source,channel,sink.</code></div>
<div class="line number10 index9 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number11 index10 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Source</code></div>
<div class="line number12 index11 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>用于接收外部源发来的数据</code></div>
<div class="line number13 index12 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number14 index13 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Channel</code></div>
<div class="line number15 index14 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>用于缓存Source发来的event,有fileChannel和memoryChannel两种,分别将event缓存于文件和内存中,当事件被sink掉,才会从channel中删除.</code></div>
<div class="line number16 index15 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number17 index16 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Sink</code></div>
<div class="line number18 index17 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>消费event,将数据发送给外部存储系统(如hdfs等),或者发送给下一个agent的source.</code></div>
</div>

<h4 id="flume+kafka+storm-kafka" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-size:14px; line-height:1.42857; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
kafka</h4>
<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-原理.1" style="margin:10px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
原理</h5>
<div class="code panel pdl conf-macro output-block" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px">

<div class="line number1 index0 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number2 index1 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number3 index2 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number5 index4 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number6 index5 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number8 index7 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>使用kafka时,我们会将消息分类,一个类别称为一个topic.</code></div>
<div class="line number9 index8 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">

<div class="line number10 index9 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>每个topic的多个partitions
 都有一个称为leader的server,用于处理分区的读写请求,</code></div>
<div class="line number11 index10 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>同时有</code><code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>0</code><code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>到多个followers
 ,用于分区备份,如果leader失败,其中任一followers变为leader.</code></div>
<div class="line number12 index11 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number13 index12 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>3</code><code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>.Producer</code></div>
<div class="line number14 index13 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>消息生产者,向topics发送数据,可以进行负载均衡,也可以定义分区函数进行分发(通过消息中的关键字,不同关键字的消息分发至不同的分区)</code></div>

 </div>
<div class="line number16 index15 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>4</code><code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>.Consumer</code></div>
<div class="line number17 index16 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>消费者,订阅消息并处理发布的消息,</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
整体架构</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
不同的producer 向kafka集群发送消息</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
不同的consumer 从kafka订阅消费消息</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<span class="confluence-embedded-file-wrapper" style="position:relative; display:inline-block; max-width:100%"><img class="confluence-embedded-image confluence-content-image-border" src="http://wiki.corp.qunar.com/confluence/download/attachments/100037148/producer_consumer.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1449754316000&amp;api=v2" alt="" style="margin:0px 2px; padding:0px; border:1px solid black; display:block"></span></p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
topic</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<span class="confluence-embedded-file-wrapper" style="position:relative; display:inline-block; max-width:100%"><img class="confluence-embedded-image confluence-content-image-border" src="http://wiki.corp.qunar.com/confluence/download/attachments/100037148/log_anatomy.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1449754321000&amp;api=v2" alt="" style="margin:0px 2px; padding:0px; border:1px solid black; display:block"></span><br>
一个topic可以有多个分区,每一个分区位于一个broker上.每一个分区都是一个顺序的、不可变的消息队列， 并且可以持续的添加.</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
同一个partition中的数据是有序的,如果要保证整topic中的消息有序,可以一个topic设置一个partition.kafka会保留所有的消息,直到消息过期.</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
消费者持有的元数据只是一个偏移量,一般情况下,当消费者处理消息的时候,偏移量会线性增加,实际上偏移量由消费者自己控制,可以回到一个先前的位置重新开始处理.</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
一个消费者的处理不会影响其他消费者对此Topic的处理.</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
并行发送,并行处理.</p>
<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-zookeeper搭建" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">

<div class="line number10 index9 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; <div class="line number72 index71 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number73 index72 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>--</code><code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>0.10</code><code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>之后的</code></div>
<div class="line number74 index73 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java spaces" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'> </code><code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>bin/kafka-configs.sh
 --zookeeper localhost:</code><code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>2181</code> <code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>--alter
 --entity-type topics --entity-name skynet_topic_td_1 --add-config retention.ms=</code><code class="java value" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,153,0)!important'>86400000</code></div>

<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-示例" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<br>
</h5>
<h4 id="flume+kafka+storm-storm" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-size:14px; line-height:1.42857; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
storm</h4>
<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-原理.2" style="margin:10px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
原理</h5>
<div class="code panel pdl conf-macro output-block" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px">
<div class="codeContent panelContent pdl" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; line-height:20px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div id="highlighter_552010" class="syntaxhighlighter sh-confluence nogutter  java" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; width:1017px; position:relative; overflow:auto; font-size:1em">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1033px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; font-size:14px; min-height:inherit'>
<tbody style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">
<tr style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">
<td class="code" style='border:0px; background:0px center; overflow:visible; font-size:14px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 15px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1018px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; min-height:inherit'>
<div class="container" title="Hint: double-click to select code" style="margin:15px 0px 0px; padding:0px 0px 15px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:relative; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:pre-wrap">
<div class="line number1 index0 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Storm是一个分布式的、高容错的实时计算系统。</code></div>
<div class="line number2 index1 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number3 index2 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>就像Hadoop提供一组通用原语来进行批量处理(batch
 processing)一样，Storm也提供了一组通用原语来进行实时计算(realtime computation)。</code></div>
<div class="line number4 index3 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number5 index4 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>storm的集群表面上看和hadoop的集群非常像。但是在Hadoop上面你运行的是MapReduce的Job,
 而在Storm上面你运行的是Topology。</code></div>
<div class="line number6 index5 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>一个关键的区别是：
 一个MapReduce Job最终会结束， 而一个Topology运永远运行（除非被显式杀掉）。</code></div>
<div class="line number7 index6 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number8 index7 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>控制节点(master
 node)</code></div>
<div class="line number9 index8 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>控制节点上面运行一个后台程序：
 Nimbus， 它的作用类似Hadoop里面的JobTracker。Nimbus负责在集群里面分布代码，分配工作给机器， 并且监控状态。</code></div>
<div class="line number10 index9 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>工作节点(worker
 node)</code></div>
<div class="line number11 index10 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>每一个工作节点上面运行一个叫做Supervisor的后台程序（类似
 TaskTracker）。Supervisor会监听分配给它那台机器的工作，根据需要 启动/关闭工作进程。</code></div>
<div class="line number12 index11 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number13 index12 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Nimbus和Supervisor之间的所有协调工作都是通过一个Zookeeper集群来完成。</code></div>
<div class="line number14 index13 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
 </div>
<div class="line number15 index14 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Woker</code></div>
<div class="line number16 index15 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Worker是Spout/Bolt中运行具体处理逻辑的进程。</code></div>
<div class="line number17 index16 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Executor</code></div>
<div class="line number18 index17 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Executor称为物理线程，每个Worker可以包含多个Executor。</code></div>
<div class="line number19 index18 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Task</code></div>
<div class="line number20 index19 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Task是具体的处理逻辑对象，默认情况下，执行器和任务对应，即一个执行器对应一个任务。</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr>

<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-搭建.1" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
搭建</h5>
<div class="code panel pdl conf-macro output-block" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px">
<div class="codeContent panelContent pdl" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; line-height:20px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div id="highlighter_188511" class="syntaxhighlighter sh-confluence nogutter  java" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; width:1017px; position:relative; overflow:auto; font-size:1em">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1017px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; font-size:14px; min-height:inherit'>
<tbody style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">
<tr style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">

<h5 id="flume+kafka+storm-Topology" style="margin:20px 0px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-size:14px; line-height:1.66667; font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
Topology</h5>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<span class="confluence-embedded-file-wrapper" style="position:relative; display:inline-block; max-width:100%"><img class="confluence-embedded-image confluence-content-image-border" src="http://wiki.corp.qunar.com/confluence/download/attachments/100037148/toplo.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1449787063000&amp;api=v2" alt="" style="margin:0px 2px; padding:0px; border:1px solid black; display:block"></span></p>
<div class="code panel pdl conf-macro output-block" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px">

<div style="margin:0px; padding:0px">

<tbody style="background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit">

<td class="code" style='border:0px; background:0px center; overflow:visible; font-size:14px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 15px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:1002px; font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; min-height:inherit'>
<div class="container" title="Hint: double-click to select code" style="margin:15px 0px 0px; padding:0px 0px 15px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:relative; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:pre-wrap">
<div class="line number1 index0 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Topology是storm的核心,我们通过编写和部署Topology来处理数据.</code></div>
<div class="line number2 index1 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>下面是一些概念.</code></div>
<div class="line number3 index2 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Stream</code></div>
<div class="line number4 index3 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Storm中的核心抽象概念就是流。流是无边界的元组(tuples)的序列。</code></div>
<div class="line number5 index4 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>通过对stream中tuple序列中每个字段命名来定义stream。</code></div>
<div class="line number6 index5 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>storm提供一些原语来分布式地、可靠地把一个stream传输进一个新的stream。(spout和bolt)</code></div>
<div class="line number7 index6 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Spout</code></div>
<div class="line number8 index7 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>spout的流的源头。</code></div>
<div class="line number9 index8 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>比如一个spout可能从kafka的topic读取消息并且把这些消息发射成一个流。</code></div>
<div class="line number10 index9 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>通常Spout会从外部数据源（队列、数据库等）读取数据，然后封装成Tuple形式，之后发送到Stream中。</code></div>
<div class="line number11 index10 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Spout是一个主动的角色，在接口内部有个nextTuple函数，Storm框架会不停的调用该函数。</code></div>
<div class="line number12 index11 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Bolt</code></div>
<div class="line number13 index12 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>bolt可以接收任意多个输入stream，作一些处理，有些bolt可能还会发射一些新的stream。</code></div>
<div class="line number14 index13 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>一些复杂的流转换，需要多个步骤，从而也就需要多个bolt。</code></div>
<div class="line number15 index14 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Bolt可以做任何事情:
 运行函数，过滤tuple,做一些聚合，做一些合并以及访问数据库等。</code></div>
<div class="line number16 index15 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Bolt是一个被动的角色，其接口中有一个execute(Tuple
 input)方法，在接收到消息之后会调用此函数，我们可以在此方法中执行自己的处理逻辑。</code></div>
<div class="line number17 index16 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>StreamGroups</code></div>
<div class="line number18 index17 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>一个Stream应如何分配数据给Bolt上面的Task.
 http:</code><code class="java comments" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; color:rgb(0,130,0)!important'>//wiki.corp.yincang.com/display/~xiao.yang/stream+groups</code></div>
<div class="line number19 index18 alt2" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>Topology</code></div>
<div class="line number20 index19 alt1" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 1em 0px 0px; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit; white-space:nowrap">
<code class="java plain" style='font-family:Consolas,"Bitstream Vera Sans Mono","Courier New",Courier,monospace; background:0px center; border:0px; bottom:auto; float:none; height:auto; left:auto; line-height:20px; margin:0px; outline:0px; overflow:visible; padding:0px; position:static; right:auto; top:auto; vertical-align:baseline; width:auto; min-height:inherit'>spout和bolt所组成一个网络会被打包成topology，
 topology是storm里面最高一级的抽象（类似 Job）， 我们可以把topology提交给storm的集群来运行.</code></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
